  - u2u_fpga_rgmii -> u2u_top_dual_bpf:u2u_top_dual_bpf .xoff_gen_0

xoff_gen_1
  - u2u_fpga_rgmii -> u2u_top_dual_bpf:u2u_top_dual_bpf .xoff_gen_1

xon_gen
  - u2u_eth_bpf -> gmac_non_aligned:gmac_non_aligned .xon_gen

xon_gen_0
  - u2u_fpga_rgmii -> u2u_top_dual_bpf:u2u_top_dual_bpf .xon_gen_0

xon_gen_1
  - u2u_fpga_rgmii -> u2u_top_dual_bpf:u2u_top_dual_bpf .xon_gen_1

y
  - lcd_sequencer -> bpf_div:bpf_div .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div1 .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div2 .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div4 .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div8 .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div16 .y
  - tb_div -> bpf_div:bpf_div32 .y
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_l_1 .y
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_r_1 .y
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_l_32 .y
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_r_32 .y

z_l_1
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_l_1 .z

z_l_32
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_l_32 .z

z_r_1
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_r_1 .z

z_r_32
  - tb_shift -> bpf_shifter:bpf_shifter_r_32 .z

{1'b0, pma_tx_dout}
  - tb_bc_pma -> alt_fifo_256x9:pma_tx2rx_fifo .data

{1'b0,reg_addr}
  - u2u_top_gm -> gmac:gmac_0 .reg_addr
  - u2u_top_gm -> gmac:gmac_1 .reg_addr
  - u2u_top -> gmac:gmac_0 .reg_addr
  - u2u_top -> gmac:gmac_1 .reg_addr

{NUM_BITS{1'b0}}
  - u2u_bist_gen -> u2u_bist_gen:LFSR_gen_u .i_Seed_Data
  - u2u_bist_rec -> u2u_bist_rec:LFSR_rec_u .i_Seed_Data

{gen_rxd_u,gen_rxd}
  - tb_pcap -> ethgenerator2:ethgenerator2 .rxd

{tmp, pma_tx2rx_q}
  - tb_bc_pma -> alt_fifo_256x9:pma_tx2rx_fifo .q

|edge_detect
  - global_reset_generator -> global_reset_generator:reset_counter_inst .reset_in

~reset_tx_clk
  - altera_tse_rgmii_module -> altera_eth_tse_std_synchronizer:U_SYNC_2 .reset_n

~rstn
  - u2u_bc_filter -> cfg_filter_mem:cfg_filter_mem_u .aclr
